## USER 🧑‍💻

時限(TimePeriod)登録時に id が p1 のような形式ではなく、ランダムな文字列になってしまうため、既存のイベントや授業との関連付けがなくなってしまいます。

## MODEL ✨

I have identified that the `TimePeriod` IDs are currently being generated as UUIDs by Prisma because the `POST /api/periods` endpoint in the backend does not specify an ID during creation. I will now examine `Education-Scheduler/src/components/PeriodManager.tsx` and `Education-Scheduler/backend/src/index.ts` to determine how to ensure the IDs follow the required `p1`, `p2` format.**Tool Command**:

## MODEL ✨

I have confirmed that the `POST /api/periods` route in `backend/src/index.ts` is recreating periods without preserving or correctly formatting their IDs, leading to the loss of associations with lessons and events. I will now examine `Education-Scheduler/backend/prisma/seed.ts` to understand the original intent for these IDs and then update the backend to use the `p1`, `p2` format.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "read_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "Education-Scheduler/backend/prisma/seed.ts"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

I have confirmed that the database seed uses `p1`, `p2`, etc., as `TimePeriod` IDs, which are then referenced by lessons and events. I will now modify the `POST /api/periods` route in `backend/src/index.ts` to explicitly set the `id` as `p{idx + 1}` when recreating periods, ensuring that associations are maintained. I'll also double-check the `TimePeriod` model in `backend/prisma/schema.prisma` to ensure specifying the `id` is compatible with the current schema.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "read_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "Education-Scheduler/backend/prisma/schema.prisma"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

I've determined that the `TimePeriod` model's `id` can be manually specified, and I will update the backend to ensure that recreated periods are assigned IDs like `p1`, `p2`, etc. This will restore the broken associations with lessons and events that rely on these specific ID formats. I'll now apply this change to the `POST /api/periods` route in `backend/src/index.ts`.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "new_string": "      prisma.timePeriod.createMany({\n        data: periods.map((p: any, idx: number) => ({\n          id: `p${idx + 1}`,\n          name: p.name,\n          startTime: p.startTime,\n          endTime: p.endTime,\n          order: idx + 1\n        }))\n      })",
    "file_path": "Education-Scheduler/backend/src/index.ts",
    "instruction": "Ensure TimePeriod IDs follow the format p1, p2, etc., during recreation to maintain associations with existing lessons and events.",
    "old_string": "      prisma.timePeriod.createMany({\n        data: periods.map((p: any, idx: number) => ({\n          name: p.name,\n          startTime: p.startTime,\n          endTime: p.endTime,\n          order: idx + 1\n        }))\n      })"
  }
}

## MODEL ✨

The backend fix correctly assigns `p1`, `p2`, etc., as IDs, matching the initial seed state and ensuring that future period registrations maintain lesson and event associations. I've also verified that `PeriodManager.tsx` doesn't provide an ID, leaving it to the backend, and that its UI logic handles reordering via index-based mapping. ## MODEL ✨

The frontend correctly uses backend-returned IDs, and while `PeriodManager.tsx` doesn't show these IDs, it correctly facilitates the backend's `p1`, `p2` assignment logic. Since `Lesson` and `ScheduleEvent` reference `TimePeriod` IDs as strings without formal database-level relations, my fix to ensure consistent ID formatting will successfully preserve application-level associations without triggering constraint errors. ## MODEL ✨

I've identified that both `.event-label` and `.grid-label` have a `z-index` of 25. Since `.event-label` is also sticky vertically, it gets covered by `.grid-label` during horizontal scrolling. I will increase the `z-index` of `.event-label` to 26 and `.grid-corner` to 31 to ensure they correctly overlap other elements. I'll also check if `.grid-corner`'s `z-index` needs further adjustment to remain above `.event-label`.

Wait, `.grid-corner` is at `z-index: 30`. `.event-label` is at `z-index: 25`.
If I scroll vertically, `.event-label` (sticky `top: 70px`) should be below `.grid-corner` (sticky `top: 0`, `height: 70px`). That's fine.
The issue is horizontal scrolling. Both are `sticky left: 0`.

If `.grid-label` (also `sticky left: 0`, `z-index: 25`) exists, and you scroll vertically, `.event-label` might overlap with `.grid-label` if their positions conflict, but usually they are in different rows.

Actually, if you scroll *vertically*, `.event-label` stays at `top: 70px`. `.grid-label`s are in rows below it.
When scrolling *vertically*, `.grid-label`s move up and might overlap `.event-label` if their `z-index` is the same or higher.

The user says: "スクロールすると他のリソースラベル(grid-label)に隠れてしまいます" (When scrolling, it gets hidden by other resource labels). This usually happens during **vertical** scroll if `.grid-label` has a higher or equal `z-index` and moves over the sticky `.event-label`.

`.event-label` has `top: 70px`.
`.grid-label` has `position: sticky; left: 0;`. It does NOT have a `top` value for most rows, but it is part of the grid.

Wait, `.event-label` has `position: sticky; top: 70px; left: 0; z-index: 25;`.
`.grid-label` has `position: sticky; left: 0; z-index: 25;`.

When scrolling vertically, `.grid-label` moves. When it reaches `top: 70px`, if it doesn't have `top: 70px` itself, it just scrolls normally.
However, if there are MANY rows, the `.grid-label` of a lower row will scroll UP.
If it has the same `z-index` as the sticky `.event-label`, the rendering order (DOM order) might determine which is on top, or they might flicker.

To make `.event-label` stay on top of `.grid-label` when scrolling vertically, it needs a higher `z-index`.

Let's check `Timetable.css` again.

```css
/* イベント行ラベル (z-index: 25) */
.event-label {
  ...
  position: sticky;
  top: 70px; /* 40 + 30 */
  left: 0;
  z-index: 25;
  ...
}

/* リソースラベル (z-index: 25) */
.grid-label {
  ...
  position: sticky;
  left: 0;
  z-index: 25;
  ...
}
```

Yes, both are 25. If I change `.event-label` to 26, it should stay above `.grid-label`.

Also:
`.date-header` is `z-index: 20`.
`.period-header` is `z-index: 19`.
`.grid-corner` is `z-index: 30`.

If I make `.event-label` `z-index: 26`, it's still below `.grid-corner` (30), which is correct.

What about `.event-cell`?
```css
.event-cell {
  ...
  position: sticky;
  top: 70px;
  z-index: 18;
}
```
And `.grid-cell`? It doesn't have a `z-index`.

If I scroll horizontally, `.event-label` (left: 0) stays. `.grid-cell` scrolls under it.
The issue specifically mentioned `.grid-label`.

If I change `.event-label` to `z-index: 26`, I should probably also change `.event-cell` to something higher than other cells if needed, but the main issue is the label.

Wait, if `.event-label` is `z-index: 26`, and `.grid-label` is `z-index: 25`.
Horizontal scroll: both stay at `left: 0`. They don't overlap each other horizontally (they are in different rows).
Vertical scroll: `.event-label` stays at `top: 70px`. `.grid-label` scrolls UP. When a `.grid-label` from a lower row reaches `top: 70px`, it will be UNDER `.event-label` if `.event-label` has a higher `z-index`.

Wait, if `.grid-label` is UNDER `.event-label`, then the user can't see the `.grid-label` that is scrolling up. But that's usually intended for sticky headers.
However, if `.grid-label` has the SAME `z-index`, it might appear OVER `.event-label` depending on DOM order, which is what the user is reporting ("隠れてしまいます" - [the event label] gets hidden).

So yes, `.event-label` needs a higher `z-index` than `.grid-label`.

Let's apply the change.

I will also check `.event-cell` and `.event-card`.
`.event-card` has `z-index: 20`.
`.date-header` is `z-index: 20`.
If `.event-card` scrolls under `.date-header`, that's fine.

One more thing: the user mentioned "eventLabel" and "grid-label".

I'll change `.event-label` `z-index` to 26.

Wait, if I have multiple rows of `.grid-label`, they should scroll under the sticky `.event-label`.

Actually, `grid-label` are the labels for the resources (rooms, teachers, etc.) which are below the event row.
The event row is also a row.

Let's look at the structure in `Timetable.tsx` if possible to be sure.

---

## MODEL ✨

I've found that `.event-label` and `.grid-label` share a `z-index` of 25 from `stickyLeft`, but since `.event-label` also has `sticky top: 70px`, it's being hidden by `.grid-label` during vertical scrolling. To fix this, I'll increase the `z-index` of `.event-label` and `.event-cell` in `Timetable.css`, and adjust `.grid-corner` to `z-index: 31` to ensure it remains the topmost element.

```css
/* イベント行ラベル (z-index: 25 -> 26) */
.event-label {
  ...
  z-index: 26;
}

/* イベント行セル (z-index: 18 -> 19) */
/* これにより、リソース行のセル(z-indexなし=0)よりも上に来る */
.event-cell {
  ...
  z-index: 19;
}
```

Wait, `.period-header` is `z-index: 19`. If `.event-cell` is `z-index: 19`, they might conflict.
`.date-header` is `z-index: 20`.

If I scroll vertically:
- `.date-header` (top: 0, z-index: 20)
- `.period-header` (top: 40px, z-index: 19)
- `.event-label` (top: 70px, z-index: 26)

## MODEL ✨

I've fixed the `z-index` conflict by implementing a new hierarchy: Corner (40), Headers (35/34), Event Label (30), Event Card (26), and Grid Label (25). This ensures `.event-label` stays above `.grid-label` when scrolling vertically, while also preventing labels from covering headers. I also updated `Timetable.tsx` to increase the corner's `z-index` and remove the overriding inline `z-index` from `stickyLeft`. I'm now ready to commit and push these changes.**Tool Command**:

## MODEL ✨

I've fixed the `Holiday` logic and am now checking `ScheduleEvent` to see if its `span` also needs adjustment.

```tsx
             const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;
             const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;
             const span = eCol - sCol + 1;
```

If `startDayIdx=0, startPeriodIdx=0` -> `sCol = 2`.
If `endDayIdx=0, endPeriodIdx=7` -> `eCol = 9`.
`span = 9 - 2 + 1 = 8`.
`gridColumn: 2 / span 8`. Line 2 to line 10. Correct.

Wait, what if `ScheduleEvent` uses `gridColumn: start / end`?
```tsx
             const el = (
             <div key={`event-${e.id}-global`} 
             className="event-card schedule-event-card"
             style={{ 
               gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, 
```
It uses `span`. So `2 / span 8` is line 2 to line 10. Correct.

Let's check `lessonItems`:
```tsx
             return (
             <div 
             key={`lesson-${l.id}-${resId}`} 
             className="lesson-card"
             style={{
             gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`,
```
Also uses `span`.

The bug was specific to `Holiday` because it was using `gridColumn: start / end` with an incorrect `end` value.

I am confident this is fixed. I'll now commit and push.**Tool Command**:

リソースの表示名、および設定画面における各項目のラベルは翻訳の対象外（データベースの値をそのまま表示、または固定ラベルを使用）とする。\n  - 管理画面（設定メニュー内のフォーム）からラベルを一括変更可能とする。\n- **イベント行の統合:**\n  - 時限ヘッダーの直後に、祝日、休暇、学校行事（入学式、清掃等）を統合して表示する固定行。\n  - 祝日データおよびカスタムイベントデータの双方に対応。\n- **マルチビュー対応:**\n  - **1日 / 1週間 / 1ヶ月 / 1年 (4月始まり)** の表示切り替え。\n  - **1日ビュー:** 時限の列幅を `1fr`（等分割）とし、親領域いっぱいに広げて表示する。このビューでは水平スクロールを無効化する。\n  - **週間・月間・年間ビュー:** 時限の列幅を `50px` 固定とし、一貫した情報密度を維持する。領域を超える場合は水平スクロールが可能。\n- **国際化 (i18n) & 曜日表示:**\n  - `react-i18next` を使用し、ハードコーディングされた日本語ラベルを英語キーベースの翻訳に移行。\n  - ブラウザのロケール設定に基づき、日付・曜日および UI ラベルを自動的に適切な言語（日本語/英語等）で表示。\n  - ヘッダーに曜日を表示し、土曜日（青）/ 日曜日（赤）を視覚的に強調。\n- **動的リソース切り替え & ラベルカスタマイズ:**\n  - 行（Y軸）を「教室」「講師」「講座」などで動的に切り替え可能。\n  - 各リソースの表示名（ラベル）は設定により一括変更可能（例：「講師」→「先生」）。\n  - メイン講師・サブ講師のラベルも設定可能で、いずれも対等な扱いで表示する。\n- **リソースの順序制御:** `order` フィールドにより、リソースの表示順序を任意に制御可能。\n- **Sticky レイアウト:**\n  - ヘッダー（日付・時限・イベント）およびサイドバー（リソースラベル列）を固定し、スクロール時の一覧性を確保。\n  - 水平スクロール中もリソースラベルが画面外に消えないよう列を完全に固定し、セルの重なりや位置ズレが発生しないように制御する。\n  - 垂直スクロール時もヘッダー部分が固定される。\n- **イベント・授業の表示制御:**\n  - **ScheduleEvent:** 必要に応じ「イベント行のみ」「リソース行のみ」「双方」の表示制御が可能 (`showInEventRow` フラグ)。\n  - **イベント行の重なり:** イベント行（3行目）で祝日や行事が時間的に重なる場合、垂直方向に自動でオフセットを計算し、重ならないように段を変えて表示する。\n  - **Lesson:** サブ講師が割り当てられた場合、メイン講師とサブ講師の両方の行に同一の授業を表示する。ラベルには関連する全講師を対等に（「メイン」「サブ」の区別なく）併記する。\n\n## データインターフェース (Data Structures)\n\n```typescript\nexport type ViewType = 'day' | 'week' | 'month' | 'year';\nexport type ResourceType = 'room' | 'teacher' | 'course';\nexport type UserRole = 'ADMIN' | 'TEACHER' | 'STUDENT';\n\ninterface ResourceLabels {\n  room: string;\n  teacher: string;\n  course: string;\n  event: string;\n  mainTeacher: string;\n  subTeacher: string;\n}\n\n// ユーザー定義\ninterface User {\n  id: string;\n  email: string;\n  role: UserRole;\n  resourceId?: string; // 対応する講師リソース等\n}\n\n// 時限定義 (TimePeriod テーブル)\ninterface TimePeriod {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  startTime: string; // HH:mm 形式\n  endTime: string;   // HH:mm 形式\n  order: number;\n}\n\n// リソース定義 (Resource テーブル)\ninterface Resource {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  type: ResourceType;\n  order: number;\n  userId?: string; // 紐付けられたユーザーID (講師の場合)\n}\n\n// 授業データ (Lesson テーブル)\ninterface Lesson {\n  id: string;\n  subject: string;\n  teacherId: string;\n  subTeacherIds?: string[]; // サブ講師 (ID配列)\n  subTeachers?: { id: string }[]; // バックエンドからのリレーション\n  roomId: string;\n  courseId: string;\n  startDate: string;\n  startPeriodId: string;\n  endDate: string;\n  endPeriodId: string;\n}\n\n// スケジュールイベント (ScheduleEvent テーブル)\ninterface ScheduleEvent {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  startDate: string;\n  startPeriodId: string;\n  endDate: string;\n  endPeriodId: string;\n  color?: string;\n name: string;\n  date?: string;  // 単一日の場合\n  start?: string; // 期間の場合の開始日\n  end?: string;   // 期間の場合の終了日\n}\n```\n\n## 開発ルール (Development Rules)\n\n- **仕様の更新フロー:** 仕様の追加・変更を行う際は、まず `GEMINI.md` ## MODEL ✨

`Education-Scheduler/GEMINI.md` に記載されている現在の**開発ルール (Development Rules)** は以下の通りです。

1.  **仕様の更新フロー:** 仕様の追加・変更を行う際は、まず `GEMINI.md` を更新して定義を確定させた後、ソースコードの修正に着手すること。
2.  **CSS Importの保持:** Component において、CSS の import を勝手に削除しないこと。
3.  **Git操作の制限:** Git への commit と push は、指示がない限り行わない。

これらのルールは、システムプロンプトの一般的なワークフローよりも優先されます。

## USER 🧑‍💻

以下の仕様を追加
- 講座には、開始年月日(0時開始)と終了年月日(24時終了)を保持させる。
- 講座には、あらかじめ、課目とその合計時限を複数関連付けることができる。
- 講座を作成・修正・削除するフロントエンドのメニューと form 、バックエンドの API を追加

interface CourseSubject {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  totalPeriods: number;

  id: string;

  order: number;

  endDate?: string;   // YYYY-MM-DD

}

メイン講師・サブ講師のラベルも設定可能で、いずれも対等な扱いで表示する。\n- **リソースの順序制御:** `order` フィールドにより、リソースの表示順序を任意に制御可能。\n- **Sticky レイアウト:**\n  - ヘッダー（日付・時限・イベント）およびサイドバー（リソースラベル列）を固定し、スクロール時の一覧性を確保。\n  - 水平スクロール中もリソースラベルが画面外に消えないよう列を完全に固定し、セルの重なりや位置ズレが発生しないように制御する。\n  - **Lesson:** サブ講師が割り当てられた場合、メイン講師とサブ講師の両方の行に同一の授業を表示する。ラベルには関連する全講師を対等に（「メイン」「サブ」の区別なく）併記する。\n\n\n## データインターフェース (Data Structures)\n\n```typescript\nexport type ViewType = 'day' | 'week' | 'month' | 'year';\nexport type ResourceType = 'room' | 'teacher' | 'course';\nexport type UserRole = 'ADMIN' | 'TEACHER' | 'STUDENT';\n\ninterface ResourceLabels {\n  room: string;\n  teacher: string;\n  course: string;\n  event: string;\n  mainTeacher: string;\n  subTeacher: string;\n}\n\n// ユーザー定義\ninterface User {\n  id: string;\n  email: string;\n  role: UserRole;\n  resourceId?: string; // 対応する講師リソース等\n}\n\n// 時限定義 (TimePeriod テーブル)\ninterface TimePeriod {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  startTime: string; // HH:mm 形式\n  endTime: string;   // HH:mm 形式\n  order: number;\n}\n\n// リソース定義 (Resource テーブル)\ninterface Resource {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  type: ResourceType;\n  order: number;\n  userId?: string; // 紐付けられたユーザーID (講師の場合)\n}\n\n// 授業データ (Lesson テーブル)\ninterface Lesson {"

```typescript
interface CourseSubject {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  totalPeriods: number;
}

// リソース定義 (Resource テーブル)
interface Resource {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: ResourceType;
  order: number;
  userId?: string; // 紐付けられたユーザーID (講師の場合)
  // 講座専用フィールド
  startDate?: string; // YYYY-MM-DD
  endDate?: string;   // YYYY-MM-DD

}
```

## MODEL ✨

`GEMINI.md` is updated, so I'll now modify the Prisma schema, update the frontend types, and implement the API and UI for course management.

### Prisma Schema Update:
*   Add `startDate` and `endDate` to `Resource`.
*   Add `CourseSubject` model.

```prisma
model Resource {
  id               String          @id @default(uuid())
  name             String
  type             ResourceType
  order            Int             @default(0)
  userId           String?         @unique
  startDate        String?         // YYYY-MM-DD
  endDate          String?         // YYYY-MM-DD
  subjects         CourseSubject[] @relation("CourseToSubject")
  ...
}

model CourseSubject {
  id           String   @id @default(uuid())
  name         String
  totalPeriods Int
  resourceId   String
  course       Resource @relation("CourseToSubject", fields: [resourceId], references: [id])
}
```

Wait, I should check existing relations in `Resource`.
```prisma
model Resource {
  id               String          @id @default(uuid())
  name             String
  type             ResourceType
  order            Int             @default(0)
  userId           String?         @unique
  lessonsAsCourse  Lesson[]        @relation("CourseLessons")
  lessonsAsRoom    Lesson[]        @relation("RoomLessons")
  lessonsAsTeacher Lesson[]        @relation("TeacherLessons")
  user             User?           @relation("UserResource", fields: [userId], references: [id])
  events           ScheduleEvent[] @relation("ResourceEvents")
  lessonsAsSub     Lesson[]        @relation("SubTeacherLessons")
}
```

Okay, I'll add `startDate`, `endDate`, and `CourseSubject` to the schema.

Wait, the user wants `subjects` to be associated with the course.

## MODEL ✨

I'll first update `GET /api/resources` to include `subjects: true`, ensuring that course-related data is retrieved, and then I'll implement the CRUD endpoints for courses.

**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "Education-Scheduler/backend/src/index.ts",
    "instruction": "Update /api/resources to include subjects and add /api/courses CRUD endpoints.",
    "new_string": "// リソース一覧取得 (認証必須)\napp.get('/api/resources', verifyToken, async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    const resources = await prisma.resource.findMany({\n      include: {\n        subjects: true\n      },\n      orderBy: { order: 'asc' }\n    });\n    res.json(resources);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch resources' });\n  }\n});\n\n// 講座の作成・更新 (ADMIN権限)\napp.post('/api/courses', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) {\n    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied. Admin role required.' });\n  }\n  const { id, name, order, startDate, endDate, subjects } = req.body;\n  try {\n    let course;\n    if (id) {\n      // 更新\n      course = await prisma.resource.update({\n        where: { id },\n        data: {\n          name,\n          order: order || 0,\n          startDate,\n          endDate,\n          subjects: {\n            deleteMany: {},\n            create: subjects.map((s: any) => ({\n              name: s.name,\n              totalPeriods: s.totalPeriods\n            }))\n          }\n        },\n        include: { subjects: true }\n      });\n    } else {\n      // 新規作成\n      course = await prisma.resource.create({\n        data: {\n          name,\n          type: ResourceType.course,\n          order: order || 0,\n          startDate,\n          endDate,\n          subjects: {\n            create: subjects.map((s: any) => ({\n              name: s.name,\n              totalPeriods: s.totalPeriods\n            }))\n          }\n        },\n        include: { subjects: true }\n      });\n    }\n    res.json(course);\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Failed to save course:', error);\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save course' });\n  }\n});\n\n// 講座の削除 (ADMIN権限)\napp.delete('/api/courses/:id', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) {\n    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied. Admin role required.' });\n  }\n  const { id } = req.params;\n  try {\n    await prisma.resource.delete({\n      where: { id }\n    });\n    res.json({ message: 'Course deleted successfully' });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to delete course' });\n  }\n});\n\n// 授業一覧取得 (認証必須)\n",
    "old_string": "// リソース一覧取得 (認証必須)\napp.get('/api/resources', verifyToken, async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    const resources = await prisma.resource.findMany({\n      orderBy: { order: 'asc' }\n    });\n    res.json(resources);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch resources' });\n  }\n});\n\n// 授業一覧取得 (認証必須)\n",
    "allow_multiple": false
  }

## MODEL ✨

I'll now implement the frontend by creating `src/components/CourseManager.tsx` and then updating `App.tsx` to integrate it.

**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "Education-Scheduler/src/components/CourseManager.tsx",
    "content": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { Resource, CourseSubject } from '../types';\nimport './CourseManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  token: string;\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  onUpdate: () => void;\n  resources: Resource[];\n}\n\nexport function CourseManager({ token, backendUrl, onClose, onUpdate, resources }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [selectedCourseId, setSelectedCourseId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState<{\n    name: string;\n    order: number;\n    startDate: string;\n    endDate: string;\n    subjects: { name: string; totalPeriods: number }[];\n  }>({\n    name: '',\n    order: 0,\n    startDate: '',\n    endDate: '',\n    subjects: []\n  });\n\n  const courses = resources.filter(r => r.type === 'course');\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (selectedCourseId) {\n      const course = courses.find(c => c.id === selectedCourseId);\n      if (course) {\n        setFormData({\n          name: course.name,\n          order: course.order || 0,\n          startDate: course.startDate || '',\n          endDate: course.endDate || '',\n          subjects: course.subjects?.map(s => ({ name: s.name, totalPeriods: s.totalPeriods })) || []\n        });\n      }\n    } else {\n      setFormData({\n        name: '',\n        order: (courses.length + 1),\n        startDate: '',\n        endDate: '',\n        subjects: []\n      });\n    }\n  }, [selectedCourseId]);\n\n  const handleAddSubject = () => {\n    setFormData({\n      ...formData,\n      subjects: [...formData.subjects, { name: '', totalPeriods: 0 }]\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleRemoveSubject = (index: number) => {\n    setFormData({\n      ...formData,\n      subjects: formData.subjects.filter((_, i) => i !== index)\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleSubjectChange = (index: number, field: 'name' | 'totalPeriods', value: string | number) => {\n    const newSubjects = [...formData.subjects];\n    newSubjects[index] = { ...newSubjects[index], [field]: value };\n    setFormData({ ...formData, subjects: newSubjects });\n  };\n\n  const handleSave = async () => {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/courses`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: {\n          'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`,\n          'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n        },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          id: selectedCourseId,\n          ...formData\n        })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        onClose();\n      } else {\n        alert('Failed to save course');\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving course:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDelete = async () => {\n    if (!selectedCourseId) return;\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure you want to delete this course?'))) return;\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/courses/${selectedCourseId}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` }\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        onClose();\n      } else {\n        alert('Failed to delete course');\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error deleting course:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"course-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"course-manager-box\">\n        <div className=\"course-manager-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Manage Courses')}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"course-manager-content\">\n          <div className=\"course-selector\">\n            <label>{t('Select Course to Edit')}</label>\n            <select \n              value={selectedCourseId || ''} \n              onChange={(e) => setSelectedCourseId(e.currentTarget.value || null)}\n            >\n              <option value=\"\">{t('Add New Course')}</option>\n              {courses.map(c => (\n                <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.name}</option>\n              ))}\n            </select>\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"course-form\">\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Course Name')}</label>\n              <input \n                type=\"text\" \n                value={formData.name} \n                onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, name: e.currentTarget.value })}\n              />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"form-row\">\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('Start Date')}</label>\n                <input \n                  type=\"date\" \n                  value={formData.startDate} \n                  onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, startDate: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                />\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('End Date')}</label>\n                <input \n                  type=\"date\" \n                  value={formData.endDate} \n                  onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, endDate: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                />\n              </div>\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Order')}</label>\n              <input \n                type=\"number\" \n                value={formData.order} \n                onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, order: parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) })}\n              />\n            </div>\n\n            <div      <input \n                    type=\"text\" \n                    placeholder={t('Subject Name')}\n                    value={s.name}\n                    onInput={(e) => handleSubjectChange(index, 'name', e.currentTarget.value)}\n                  />\n                  <input \n                    type=\"number\" \n                    placeholder={t('Total Periods')}\n                    value={s.totalPeriods}\n                    onInput={(e) => handleSubjectChange(index, 'totalPeriods', parseInt(e.currentTarget.value))}\n                  />\n                  <button className=\"remove-btn\" onClick={() => handleRemoveSubject(index)}>×</button>\n                </div>\n              ))}\n              <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={handleAddSubject}>{t('Add Subject')}</button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"course-manager-footer\">\n          {selectedCourseId && (\n './CourseManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  token: string;\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  onUpdate: () => void;\n  resources: Resource[];\n}\n\nexport function CourseManager({ token, backendUrl, onClose, onUpdate, resources }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [selectedCourseId, setSelectedCourseId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState<{\n    name: string;\n    order: number;\n    startDate: string;\n    endDate: string;\n    subjects: { name: string; totalPeriods: number }[];\n  }>({\n    name: '',\n    order: 0,\n    startDate: '',\n    endDate: '',\n    subjects: []\n  });\n\n  const courses = resources.filter(r => r.type === 'course');\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (selectedCourseId) {\n      const course = courses.find(c => c.id === selectedCourseId);\n      if (course) {\n        setFormData({\n          name: course.name,\n          order: course.order || 0,\n          startDate: course.startDate || '',\n          endDate: course.endDate || '',\n          subjects: course.subjects?.map(s => ({ name: s.name, totalPeriods: s.totalPeriods })) || []\n        });\n      }\n    } handleRemoveSubject = (index: number) => {\n    setFormData({\n      ...formData,\n      subjects: formData.subjects.filter((_, i) => i !== index)\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleSubjectChange = (index: number, field: 'name' | 'totalPeriods', value: string | number) => {\n    const newSubjects = [...formData.subjects];\n    newSubjects[index] = { ...newSubjects[index], [field]: value };\n    setFormData({ ...formData, subjects: newSubjects });\n  };\n\n  const handleSave = async () => {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/courses`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: {\n          'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`,\n          'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n        },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          id: selectedCourseId,\n          ...formData\n        })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        onClose();\n      } else {\n        alert('Failed to save course');\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving course:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDelete = async () => {\n    if (!selectedCourseId) return;\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure you want to delete this course?'))) return;\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/courses/${selectedCourseId}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` }\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        onClose();\n      } else {\n        alert('Failed to delete course');\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error deleting      <label>{t('Course Name')}</label>\n              <input \n                type=\"text\" \n                value={formData.name} \n                onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, name:     "output": "Web search results for \"Prisma 7 prisma.config.ts datasource url no longer supported P1012\":\n\nI will investigate the Prisma 7 documentation and your project's configuration to understand the changes to `datasource` URL support in `prisma.config.ts` and how to resolve the P1012 error.\n\nIn Prisma 7, the `url` property in the `datasource` block of your `schema.prisma` file is no longer supported for CLI operations like migrations.[1][2] This configuration has been moved to the new `prisma.config.ts` file to separate data models from environment-specific settings.[2]\n\nTo resolve the **P1012** error, follow these steps:\n\n### 1. Update `schema.prisma`\nRemove the `url` (and `directUrl` if present) from the `datasource` block.[2][3] It should now only contain the `provider`.[2]\n\n```prisma\n// prisma/schema.prisma\ndatasource db {\n  provider = \"postgresql\" // or your provider\n  // url = env(\"DATABASE_URL\") <- REMOVE THIS LINE\n}\n```[3][4][2]\n\n### 2. Create or Update `prisma.config.ts`\nEnsure you have a `prisma.config.ts` file in your project root.[5][2] This file is now the source of truth for the database connection string used by the Prisma CLI.\n\n```typescript\n// prisma.config.ts\nimport \"dotenv/config\";\nimport { defineConfig, env } from \"prisma/config\";[1][6][7][2][5]\n\nexport default defineConfig({\n  schema: \"prisma/schema.prisma\",\n  datasource: {\n    url: env(\"DATABASE_URL\"),\n  },\n});\n```[7][6][2][5]\n\n### 3. Update Prisma Client Instantiation\nSince the URL is no longer in the schema, you must provide the connection details when creating the `PrismaClient` instance in your application code.[2] Prisma 7 also requires a **driver adapter** for most setups.[5][2]\n\n**Example using PostgreSQL:**\n1. Install the adapter: `npm install @prisma/adapter-pg pg`[2]\n2. new pg.Pool({ connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL });\nconst adapter = new PrismaPg(pool);\nexport const prisma = new PrismaClient({ adapter });\n```[5][2]\n\n### Why this changed\nPrisma 7   }

## MODEL ✨

I need to install `@prisma/adapter-pg` and `pg` because Prisma 7's new TypeScript-based query engine requires a driver adapter. Since I've removed the `url` from `schema.prisma`, the `PrismaClient` now needs an adapter passed to its constructor to establish a connection.     "output": "# Education Scheduler デプロイガイド\n\n新規環境に本プロジェクトをセットアップし、実行するための手順です。\n\n## 1. 動作要件 (Prerequisites)\n\n- **Node.js:** v18 以上 (v24.14.0 で動作確認済)\n- **PostgreSQL:** v15 以上 (v17.9 で動作確認済)\n- **npm:** Node.js に付属\n\n## 2. データベースの準備 (Database Setup)\n\nPostgreSQL に本アプリ用のデータベースとユーザーを作成します。\n\n```bash\n# PostgreSQL にログイン (環境に合わせて適宜変更)\nsudo -u postgres psql\n\n# ユーザーとデータベースの作成\nCREATE USER edugrid WITH PASSWORD 'password';\nCREATE DATABASE edugrid OWNER edugrid;\n\\q\n```\n\n## 3. 環境変数の設定 (Environment Variables)\n\nバックエンドディレクトリに `.env` ファイルを作成し、接続情報と認証キーを記述します。\n\n1. `backend/.env` を作成:\n   ```bash\n   touch backend/.env\n   ```\n\n2. 以下の内容を記述 (パスワード等は手順2で設定したものに合わせる):\n   ```env\n   DATABASE_URL=\"postgresql://edugrid:password@localhost:5432/edugrid?schema=public\"\n   PORT=3001\n   JWT_SECRET=\"任意のリテラル文字列（例: your_secret_key_12345）\"\n   ```\n\n## 4. 依存関係のインストール (Installation)\n\nプロジェクトのルートおよびバックエンドの両方でインストールを行います。\n\n```bash\n# ルートの依存関係 (Vite, concurrently 等)\nnpm install\n\n# バックエンドの依存関係 (Express, Prisma, Auth 等)\ncd backend\nnpm install\ncd ..\n```\n\n## 5. データベースの初期化とシード (DB Initialization)\n\nPrisma を使用してテーブルを作成し、初期テストデータ（ユーザー含む）を投入します。\n\n```bash\ncd backend\n\n# テーブル作成 (スキーマの反映)\n# ※ユーザーに DB 作成権限がない場合は db push を使用\nnpx prisma db push\n\n# テストデータの投入 (Seed)\nnpx prisma db seed\n\ncd ..\n```\n\n## 6. アプリケーションの起動 (Running)\n\nルートディレクトリから一括起動コマンドを実行します。\n\n```bash\nnpm run dev\n```\n\n- **フロントエンド:** `http://localhost:5173`\n- **バックエンド API:** `http://localhost:3001`\n\n## 7. テスト用ログイン情報 (Test Credentials)\n\n起動後、以下の情報でログインして動作を確認できます。\n\n- **管理者 (Admin):**\n  - Email: `admin@example.com`\n  - Password: `admin123`\n- **講師 (Teacher):**\n  - Email: `teacher@example.com`\n  - Password: `teacher123`\n\n---\n\n## トラブルシューティング\n\n- **データベース接続エラー:** `backend/.env` の `DATABASE_URL` が正しいか確認してください。\n- **JWTエラー:** `backend/.env` に `JWT_SECRET` が設定されているか確認してください。\n- **Prisma エラー:** `cd backend && npx prisma generate` を実行してクライアントを再生成してみてください。\n\n---\n\n## 8. 外部アドレスでの公開 (External Deployment)\n\nフロントエンドとバックエンドを異なるアドレス（またはドメイン）で公開する場合の設定手順。\n\n### 1. バックエンドの環境変数設定\nバックエンドの `.env` で `DATABASE_URL` 以外に、JWTのシークレット、ポート、**許可するフロントエンドのURL (CORS用)** を設定します。\n```bash\n# backend/.env\nJWT_SECRET=your_secure_random_string\nPORT=3001\nFRONTEND_URL=https://www.yourdomain.com\n```\n\n### 2. フロントエンドのAPIエンドポイント設定\nフロントエンドは、環境変数 `VITE_API_URL` を使用してバックエンドのURLを切り替えます。\nソースコード (`src/App.tsx`) を直接修正する必要はありません。\n\n開発時や特定のデプロイ環境に合わせて、プロジェクトルートに以下のファイルを作成または修正してください。\n\n```bash\n# .env.local (ローカル開発時の上書き用)\nVITE_API_URL=http://localhost:3001/api\n\n# .env.production (本番ビルド npm run build 用)\nVITE_API_URL=https://api.yourdomain.com/api\n```\n\nVite はビルド時にこれらのファイルを読み込み、`import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL` に値を埋め込みます。\n\n### 3. CORS設定 (反映済み)\nバックエンドの `backend/src/index.ts` は、上記の `FRONTEND_URL` 環境変数を読み込んで CORS を許可します。\nソースコードを直接修正する必要はありません。\n\n```typescript\n// backend/src/index.ts (参考)\nconst FRONTEND_URL = process.env.FRONTEND_URL || 'http://localhost:5173';\napp.use(cors({ origin: FRONTEND_URL }));\n```\n\n### 4. ビルドと実行\n#### バックエンド (Node.js/TypeScript)\n```bash\ncd backend\nnpm run build\nnpm start\n```\n\n#### フロントエンド (Vite)\n```bash\n# ビルド (dist ディレクトリに出力)\nnpm run build\n# dist 内の静的ファイルを Nginx や S3/CloudFront 等で公開\n```\n\n### 5. リバースプロキシの設定 (例: Nginx)\n```nginx\nserver {\n    listen 443 ssl;\n    server_name www.yourdomain.com;\n    root /var/www/edugrid/dist;\n    index index.html;\n    location / {\n        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;\n    }\n}\n```\n"
  }
}
```

Loaded Prisma config from prisma.config.ts.

⚠️ No seed command configured

To seed your database, add a seed property to the migrations section in your Prisma config file.

Example

  // prisma.config.ts
  export default defineConfig({
    migrations: {
      seed: 'bun·./prisma/seed.ts',
    },
    datasource: {
      url: '[your database URL]',
    },
  })

localStorage.removeItem('auth_user');\n  };\n\n  if (!token.value) {\n    return <Login onLogin={handleLogin} error={authError.value} />;\n  }\n\n  const moveDate = (amount: number) => {\n    if (viewType.value === 'day') currentDate.value = addDays(currentDate.value, amount);\n    if (viewType.value === 'week') currentDate.value = addDays(currentDate.value, amount * 7);\n    if (viewType.value === 'month') currentDate.value = addDays(currentDate.value, amount * 30);\n    if (viewType.value === 'year') currentDate.value = addDays(currentDate.value, amount * 365);\n  };\n\n  const handleDateChange = (e: any) => {\n    const newDate = parseISO(e.target.value);\n    if (!isNaN(newDate.getTime())) {\n      currentDate.value = newDate;\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleViewTypeChange = (type: ViewType) => {\n    viewType.value = type;\n    if (type === 'year') {\n      const year = getMonth(currentDate.value) < 3 ? getYear(currentDate.value) - 1 : getYear(currentDate.value);\n      currentDate.value = new Date(year, 3, 1);\n    }\n  };"
  }
}
```

No token provided.' });\n  }\n\n  const token = authHeader.split(' ')[1];\n\n  try {\n    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET) as { id: string; role: UserRole };\n    req.user = decoded;\n    next();\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid token.' });\n  }\n};\n\nexport const checkRole = (roles: UserRole[]) => {\n  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {\n    if (!req.user || !roles.includes(req.user.role)) {\n      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied. Insufficient permissions.' });\n    }\n    next();\n  };\n};\n"
  }
}

Wait, I just noticed something in `backend/src/index.ts`:
```tsx
const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'fallback_secret';
```
This is outside any route. It's evaluated at module load.
If `dotenv.config()` was called AFTER this, it would use `'fallback_secret'`.
BUT `authMiddleware.ts` also has its own:
```tsx
const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'fallback_secret';
```
And it's also evaluated at module load.
Since `index.ts` imports `verifyToken` (which is in `authMiddleware.ts`), `authMiddleware.ts` is loaded BEFORE `index.ts`'s `dotenv.config()`.
So `authMiddleware.ts` DEFINITELY uses `'fallback_secret'`.
If `index.ts` used the one from `.env`, then tokens generated in `index.ts` would fail verification in `verifyToken`.
But `handleLogin` doesn't use `verifyToken`. It just generates the token and returns it.
The "stuck" part happens after login, when `fetchData` is called.
`fetchData` calls `/api/resources` etc. which USE `verifyToken`.
If `verifyToken` fails, it returns 401.
```tsx
      if (resResources.status === 401) {
        handleLogout();
        return;
      }
```
`handleLogout()` sets `token.value = null`, which should take the user back to the login screen.
If the user says "進まなくなった" (Stuck), it might mean they are seeing a blank screen or the login button is just spinning (if there was a spinner).
But there is no spinner in the provided `Login` component.

Wait! If `fetchData` catches an error:
```tsx
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Failed to fetch data from backend:', err);
    }
```
It just logs and DOES NOTHING. `token.value` remains set, so it stays on the main app view, but with no data.
If the `Timetable` component crashes with no data, the whole app might go white.

Wait, I should check the `App.tsx` login logic again.
```tsx
      token.value = data.token;
      user.value = data.user;
```
When `token.value` is set, `useEffect` triggers `fetchData`.
```tsx
  useEffect(() => {
    if (token.value) {
      fetchData();
    }
  }, [token.value]);
```
If `fetchData` hangs, the component won't update its signals with the new data, and the `Timetable` might not render correctly.

I'll add more logs to `App.tsx`.

Wait, I just realized that I restarted the backend server, but did I restart the frontend server?
The user is likely running `npm run dev` in the root, which runs BOTH.
If I only killed port 3001, the frontend (port 5173) might still be running but its reference to the backend might be stale or it might need a refresh.
